### [1] [Quasi-affine schemes and singly compactly generated $t$-structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19417)
*Giovanni Rossanigo*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文证明了对于具有充足线束族的拟紧拟分离概形X，其拟凝聚层导出∞-范畴上标准t-结构的连通半部QCoh(X)≥0由一个连通完美对象紧生成当且仅当X是拟仿射的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究拟凝聚层导出范畴中连通半部的紧生成性质与概形几何性质之间的关系，特别是探究何种概形条件下该连通半部可由单个连通完美对象生成。

Method: 利用拟凝聚层导出∞-范畴的标准t-结构及其连通半部的紧生成性，结合概形的拟紧拟分离性和充足线束族条件，通过严谨的范畴论与代数几何论证建立等价刻画。

Result: QCoh(X)≥0由一个连通完美对象紧生成当且仅当X是拟仿射概形。

Conclusion: 该结果给出了拟凝聚层范畴连通半部具有强紧生成性质的几何刻画，揭示了概形的拟仿射性与其导出范畴的生成性之间的深刻联系。

Abstract: We show that for a quasi-compact quasi-separated scheme $X$ with an ample family of line bundles, the connective half $\text{QCoh}(X)_{\geq0}$ of the standard $t$-structure on the derived $\infty$-category of quasi-coherent sheaves is compactly generated by a connective perfect object if and only if $X$ is quasi-affine.

</details>


### [2] [Calculating Archimedean Height Pairing via generalized cross-ratio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19997)
*Alexander B. Goncharov*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文计算了射影空间中平面的一种广义交比，该交比源于Bloch提出的阿基米德高度配对在算术维度互补的同调平凡环之间的类比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Spencer Bloch强调，两个算术维度互补的同调平凡环之间的阿基米德高度配对（或双扩张中的相关类）应能产生经典交比的有趣类比，本文旨在计算这种广义交比在射影空间平面情形下的具体形式。

Method: 本文通过阿基米德高度配对理论，对射影空间中特定维度的平面构造广义交比，并进行了具体计算。

Result: 成功计算了射影空间中平面的广义交比。

Conclusion: 本文为Bloch提出的广义交比猜想在射影空间平面情形下提供了具体实例和计算结果。

Abstract: During the last several years, Spencer Bloch emphasized that Archimedean hight pairings between two homologically trivial cycles of complimentary arithmetic dimensions, or the closely related classes in the biextension, should lead to interesting analogs of the classical cross ratio. In this note I calculate such a generalized cross-ratio for planes in the projective space.

</details>


### [3] [A simple proof for Hochster's Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20016)
*Stefan Schröer*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文给出了Hochster定理的一个概念性证明，该定理断言每个谱空间都同胚于某个环的谱。通过将环构造为素有限环的滤过直接极限，并利用有限Kolmogoroff空间的组合（余等化子和一维空间的推出）以及Schwede关于环笛卡尔方块中素理想的观察，简化了Ershov的论证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为Hochster定理（每个谱空间同胚于某环的谱）提供一个更简洁、概念性的证明，并简化Ershov此前沿着这一思路的论证。

Method: 给定一个基域和一个谱空间，将环构造为素有限环的滤过直接极限，这些素有限环以函子方式依赖于有限Kolmogoroff空间。关键步骤包括：利用余等化子和一维空间的推出对有限Kolmogoroff空间进行组装，并结合Schwede关于环笛卡尔方块中素理想的观察。

Result: 成功给出了Hochster定理的一个概念性证明，简化了Ershov的论证。

Conclusion: 通过有限Kolmogoroff空间的范畴论组合和Schwede的观察，提供了一种更简洁、更概念化的方式证明每个谱空间都是某个环的谱。

Abstract: We give a conceptual proof for Hochster's Theorem, which asserts that each spectral space is homeomorphic to the spectrum of a ring. Given a ground field and a spectral space, our ring is constructed as filtered direct limit of prime-finite ring, which are attached in a functorial way to finite Kolmogoroff spaces. The construction simplifies an argument of Ershov along these lines. Our crucial ingredient is an assembly of finite Kolmogoroff spaces in terms of coequalizers and pushouts of one-dimensional spaces, and Schwede's observation on prime ideals in cartesian squares of rings.

</details>


### [4] [Spectral and Logarithmic Atiyah Classes for Higgs Bundles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20154)
*Pradip Kumar,Sai Rasmi Ranjan Mohanty,Savita Rani,Rahul Kumar Singh*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文证明了在光滑谱曲线上，正则半单Higgs丛的Atiyah类由谱线丛的Atiyah类诱导，并取值于Higgs场的中心化子中；当判别式可约时，进一步构造了分支除子上的对数细化，使Atiyah类延拓为具有对数奇点且取值于正则化中心化子层的类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解正则半单Higgs丛的几何结构，特别是其Atiyah类与谱线丛Atiyah类之间的关系，并解决分支除子处Atiyah类的奇点问题。

Method: 利用光滑谱曲线上的代数几何方法，通过分析Atiyah类在étale locus上的诱导关系，并在判别式可约时引入对数极点的细化构造和正则化中心化子层。

Result: 证明了在étale locus上Atiyah类由谱线丛Atiyah类诱导且取值于中心化子；在判别式可约时，构造了对数细化，得到具有对数极点且取值于正则化中心化子层的延拓类。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了Higgs丛Atiyah类与谱线丛Atiyah类之间的精确联系，并提供了分支除子处的对数延拓，深化了对Higgs丛模空间几何的理解。

Abstract: For a regular semisimple Higgs bundle with a smooth spectral curve, we prove that, over the \etale\ locus, the Atiyah class of the underlying bundle is induced by the Atiyah class of the spectral line bundle and takes values in the centralizer of the Higgs field. Further, when the discriminant is reduced, we construct a logarithmic refinement across the branch divisor: the Atiyah class extends as a class with logarithmic poles and values in a natural regularized centralizer sheaf.

</details>


### [5] [Wild automorphisms and compound isotriviality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20228)
*Jason Bell,Rahim Moosa*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文在特征零的差域模型论启发下，引入了“复合基本等向性”自同构概念，并证明了Reichstein-Rogalski-Zhang的“野性自同构猜想”对该类动力系统成立：射影不可约簇上若存在复合基本等向性的野性自同构，则该簇必为阿贝尔簇。同时给出了该猜想在非自治σ-簇情形下的反例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受特征零差域模型论启发，旨在研究代数簇上的自同构动力系统分类，特别是证明或证伪Reichstein、Rogalski和Zhang提出的“野性自同构猜想”。

Method: 引入“复合基本等向性”(compound fundamental isotrivial)自同构概念——通过有限步等变纤维化从（可能非自治的）代数动力系统构造，该系统在基扩张后平凡化。利用模型论与代数几何工具进行分析。

Result: 证明了所有阿贝尔簇上的野性自同构是复合基本等向性的；反之，射影不可约簇上若存在复合基本等向性的野性自同构，则该簇必为阿贝尔簇。此外，构造了非自治σ-簇情形下该猜想的反例。

Conclusion: 针对复合基本等向性动力系统，证明了野性自同构猜想成立，明确了其适用边界；同时指出该猜想不能直接推广到非自治σ-簇情形。

Abstract: Inspired by the model theory of difference fields in characteristic zero, a class of automorphisms of an algebraic variety, here called compound fundamental isotrivial, is introduced. These are algebraic dynamical systems that are built up via a finite sequence of equivariant fibrations from (possibly nonautonomous) algebraic dynamics which trivialise after base extension over themselves. Every wild automorphism of an abelian variety is compound fundamental isotrivial. Conversely, it is shown that the only irreducible projective varieties admitting a wild automorphism that is compound fundamental isotrivial are the abelian varieties. That is, the wild automorphism conjecture of Reichstein, Rogalski, and Zhang is here proven for compound fundamental isotrivial dynamics. Along the way, a counterexample to the naive generalisation of the conjecture to the nonautonomous setting of $σ$-varieties is provided.

</details>


### [6] [Anti-Zariski pairs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20268)
*Peng Ren,Eugenii Shustin*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文提出"反Zariski对"概念：两条曲线嵌入平面后拓扑同胚，但属于等奇异族的不同分支，并给出实例及相关讨论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Zariski对描述的是同度同奇异型但拓扑不同的曲线对，本文从反向视角出发，探索拓扑同胚但属于不同等奇异族分支的曲线对，以丰富对等奇异族与拓扑之间关系的理解。

Method: 定义"反Zariski对"概念，通过构造具体例子展示这种对的存在性，并围绕相关理论问题展开讨论。

Result: 成功构造出反Zariski对的实例，证明存在拓扑等价但属于不同等奇异族分支的曲线对。

Conclusion: 反Zariski对的发现揭示了等奇异族结构与拓扑结构之间更复杂的对应关系，为进一步研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: In 1929, O. Zariski found a pair of complex plane algebraic curves of the same degree and with the same collection of singularities, but embedded into the plane in a topologically different way. Accordingly, such curves belong to different components of the equisingular family. This phenomenon has been intensively studied till now. In this note, we propose a different insight on this subject: Two curves $C',C''\subset\PP^2$ form an {\it anti-Zariski pair}, if $(\PP^2,C')$ and $(\PP^2,C'')$ are homeomorhic, but $C'$ and $C''$ belong to different components of the equisingular family. We exhibit examples of anti-Zariski pairs and discuss related issues.

</details>


### [7] [Symplectic duality for the constant term of the geometric Eisenstein series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20277)
*Igor Chaban*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个拟映射空间的某种上同调，它范畴化了函数域上几何Eisenstein级数的常数项。该上同调带有一个对应代数的作用，其交换子代数是Coulomb分支（即A_n曲面奇点）上的正则函数环。秩一局部系统诱导了Coulomb分支上的平展基本群作用，其概形论不动点带上一个自然向量丛。主要结果将拟映射空间的上同调与这个向量丛的局部上同调在参数一般范围内等同起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 范畴化几何Eisenstein级数的常数项，并建立拟映射空间上同调与Coulomb分支上向量丛局部上同调之间的联系。

Method: 研究拟映射空间的上同调结构，分析对应代数作用及其交换子代数与Coulomb分支（A_n曲面奇点）的关系；利用秩一局部系统诱导的平展基本群作用构造不动点上的向量丛，并通过比较拟映射空间上同调与向量丛局部上同调来建立主要结论。

Result: 在参数一般范围内，拟映射空间的上同调与Coulomb分支不动点处向量丛的局部上同调相等。

Conclusion: 建立了拟映射空间上同调与Coulomb分支几何之间的深层联系，为几何表示论中Eisenstein级数的范畴化提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study the cohomology of a quasimap space that categorifies the constant term of the geometric Eisenstein series for the mirabolic parabolic subgroup of $GL$ over the function field $\mathbb{F}_q(C)$ of a smooth projective curve $C$. This cohomology carries a natural action of an algebra of correspondences whose commutative subalgebra is the ring of regular functions on the Coulomb branch, which here is the $A_{n}$-surface singularity. A choice of rank-one local system on $C$ induces an action of the étale fundamental group on the Coulomb branch; the scheme-theoretic fixed locus carries a natural vector bundle. Our main result identifies the cohomology of the quasimap space with the local cohomology of this vector bundle, for a generic range of parameters.

</details>


### [8] [Plane curve singularities and Fitting ideals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20343)
*Alexandru Dimca,Gabriel Sticlaru*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究非拟齐次平面曲线奇点的Tjurina理想所关联的Fitting理想，重点关注Milnor数与Tjurina数之差不超过2时的特殊性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究非拟齐次平面曲线奇点中Tjurina理想与Fitting理想之间的代数结构关系，特别是当Milnor数与Tjurina数之差较小时出现的特殊代数性质。

Method: 通过代数几何与交换代数方法，分析非拟齐次平面曲线奇点的Tjurina理想，研究其Fitting理想的代数结构，并考虑Milnor数与Tjurina数之差的约束条件。

Result: 发现当Milnor数与Tjurina数之差不超过2时，非拟齐次平面曲线奇点的Tjurina理想所关联的Fitting理想具有特殊的代数性质。

Conclusion: Milnor数与Tjurina数之差的特定取值（≤2）对非拟齐次平面曲线奇点的Fitting理想结构有显著影响，揭示了奇点分类的代数特征。

Abstract: In this note we investigate the Fitting ideals associated to the Tjurina ideal of a non quasi-homogeneous plane curve singularity. Special properties occur when the difference between Milnor number and Tjurina number is at most 2.

</details>


### [9] [On Ziegler pairs of line arrangements: from non-existence to abundance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20421)
*Alexandru Dimca,Piotr Pokora*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文从数值与同调两个角度研究线排列的Ziegler对。首先证明当线条数d<9时，交格决定了所考虑的指数数据；随后列出d=10时的六个不同的Ziegler对。特别地，构造了高阶例子，这些例子具有相同的交格、相同的雅可比关系最小次数、相同的Milnor代数Hilbert函数，但具有不同的极小分次自由分解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索线排列的Ziegler对中，交格、指数数据、雅可比关系、Milnor代数Hilbert函数与极小分次自由分解之间的依赖关系，寻找在多个数值不变量相同的情况下仍能区分不同排列的同调不变量。

Method: 采用数值与同调双重视角分析线排列。对于d<9的情况通过计算验证交格决定指数数据；对于d=10的情况列举六个Ziegler对。在高阶构造中，固定交格、雅可比关系最小次数和Milnor代数Hilbert函数，分析极小分次自由分解的差异。

Result: 当d<9时，交格完全决定了所考虑的指数数据；发现了六个d=10的Ziegler对；成功构造了高阶例子，其中交格、雅可比关系最小次数、Milnor代数Hilbert函数均相同，但极小分次自由分解不同。

Conclusion: 线排列的某些数值不变量（如指数数据）在d<9时完全由交格决定，但同调不变量（如极小分次自由分解）可以在其他数值不变量相同的情况下提供额外的区分能力，这为理解Ziegler对的本质提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study Ziegler pairs of line arrangements from both numerical and homological perspectives. First, we show that for arrangements of $d<9$ lines the intersection lattice determines the exponent data considered here. Then we list six distinct Ziegler pair with $d=10$. In particular, we construct higher-degree examples with the same intersection lattice, the same minimal degree of a Jacobian relation, and the same Hilbert function of the Milnor algebra, but with different minimal graded free resolutions.

</details>


### [10] [Eigenvector Varieties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20432)
*Sandra Di Rocco,Bernd Sturmfels,Svala Sverrisdóttir*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了方阵线性空间关联的特征向量簇，特别关注李代数与量子系统哈密顿量的情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对任意方阵线性空间，其关联的特征向量簇（由该空间中矩阵的特征向量构成）缺乏系统性研究，尤其是在李代数量子系统哈密顿量等具有重要物理与数学意义的背景下。

Method: 采用代数几何与表示论的方法，对一般线性空间的特征向量簇进行定义与分类，并针对李代数及量子哈密顿量的具体结构进行专门分析。

Result: 建立了特征向量簇的代数几何性质，揭示了其在李代数与量子系统哈密顿量框架下的具体结构与特征。

Conclusion: 特征向量簇为理解线性空间（尤其是李代数和量子哈密顿量）的特征值问题提供了新的几何视角，具有进一步推广的理论价值。

Abstract: Any linear space of square matrices has an associated eigenvector variety. Its points are eigenvectors of matrices from that linear space. We present a systematic study of eigenvector varieties, with focus on Lie algebras and Hamiltonians of quantum systems.

</details>


### [11] [Étale and Quasicoherent Cohomological Dimensions of Subspace Arrangements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20448)
*Manolis C. Tsakiris,Matteo Varbaro*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文报告了在étale上同调维数与拟凝聚上同调维数之间关系的研究进展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索étale上同调与拟凝聚上同调这两个重要上同调理论在维数上的内在联系，以深化对代数几何中上同调现象的理解。

Method: 采用工作进展中的理论分析方法，研究两种上同调维数的关系。

Result: 尚未给出最终结果，属于阶段性研究报告。

Conclusion: 该工作仍在进行中，未来可能会建立两种上同调维数之间的精确关系。

Abstract: We report some work in progress on the relationship between étale and quasicoherent cohomological dimensions.

</details>

# math.AT [[Back]](#toc)

### [12] [The Kernel of the $\hat A$-Genus in Rational Spin Bordism is Generated by Ricci-Positive Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19505)
*Gerald Höhn,Philipp Höhn*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 本文证明，在有理Spin配边中，具有正Ricci曲率度量的流形所代表的配边类恰好张成$\hat A$-示性数核。通过构造奇数次二次曲面的光滑完全交集（Fano流形），并利用$\hat A$-示性数的一阶加厚诱导的线性泛函与多项式插值论证，证明了该满秩性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回答复椭圆属背景下提出的关于正Ricci曲率有理配边障碍的问题，即在微分有理Spin范畴中刻画哪些配边类可由正Ricci曲率流形表示。

Method: 构造奇数次（$\ell=1,3,\ldots,2m-1$）二次曲面的光滑完全交集$Y_{m,\ell}\subset\mathbb{CP}^{2m+\ell}$（实维$4m$，Spin且Fano，具有正Ricci曲率）。通过$\hat A$-示性数的一阶加厚诱导$m-1$个$(J/J^2)_{4m}$上的线性泛函，其在$[Y_{m,\ell}]$上的取值由严格递增次数的多项式$P_{m,q}(\ell)$控制，最后用多项式插值证明满秩。

Result: 在每一度上，正Ricci曲率Spin流形的有理配边类的$\mathbb{Q}$-张成空间恰好等于$\hat A$-示性数的核$J=\ker(\hat A:R\to\mathbb{Q}[u])$。

Conclusion: 完全解决了有理Spin配边中正Ricci曲率流形的配边类刻画问题，证实该核中每个有理类均可由正Ricci曲率流形实现。

Abstract: We prove that, in every degree, the rational Spin bordism classes represented by manifolds admitting metrics with positive Ricci curvature span exactly the kernel of the $\hat A$-genus. More precisely, for \[ R=Ω_*^{Spin}\otimes\mathbb{Q},\qquad J=\ker(\hat A:R\longrightarrow\mathbb{Q}[u]),\] the $\mathbb{Q}$-span of bordism classes of Ricci-positive Spin manifolds equals $J$ in each degree. This answers, in the differentiable rational Spin category, a question about rational bordism obstructions to positive Ricci curvature which was raised in the context of complex elliptic genera.
  The proof uses smooth complete intersections of an odd number $\ell$ of quadrics \[ Y_{m,\ell}\subset \mathbb{CP}^{2m+\ell}, \qquad \ell=1,\, 3,\, \ldots,\, 2m-1. \] These manifolds have real dimension $4m$, are Spin and Fano, and therefore admit metrics with positive Ricci curvature. A first-order thickening of the $\hat A$-genus induces $m-1$ linear functionals on $(J/J^2)_{4m}$. Their values on the classes $[Y_{m,\ell}]$ are governed by polynomials $P_{m,q}(\ell)$ of strictly increasing degrees $q+1=1$, $2$, $\ldots$, $m-1$. This gives full rank by a polynomial-interpolation argument.

</details>


### [13] [$K$-Theoretic Obstructions to Linearizing QCA Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19657)
*Mattie Ji,Bowen Yang*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子细胞自动机（QCA）表示的线性化问题，通过代数K-理论谱发展了障碍理论，并在复数域上完全计算了点、线和平面上的QCA空间同伦类型。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用作者先前构造的QCA代数K-理论谱，发展了一套障碍理论，通过QCA空间的同伦类型提取普适的线性化障碍类。

Result: 在复数代数与酉情形下，完全计算了点、线和平面上的QCA空间同伦类型。

Abstract: Projective representations arise naturally in physics and representation theory, and determining whether they can be linearized has been a fundamental problem. In this work, we study the analogous problem for quantum cellular automata (QCA) representations, which incorporate locality constraints imposed by a metric space $X$. Over an arbitrary field $\mathbb{F}$, we develop an obstruction theory for the linearization of QCA representations, using the algebraic $K$-theory spectrum of QCA constructed in previous work of the authors. The resulting obstructions are governed by the homotopy type of the QCA spaces, from which we extract universal obstruction classes to linearization. In the complex algebraic and unitary case, we also fully compute the homotopy types of the QCA spaces over a point, a line, and a plane.

Abstract: In the presented article, the next-to-the-leading-order calculation of the differential cross-section of the Compton scattering subprocess $qg \rightarrow qγ$ for prompt photon production in proton-proton collisions at NICA energies has been carried out, both without and taking into account the longitudinal polarization of colliding protons.
  It is shown that the contribution of the next-to-leading order to the differential cross-section is significant at high energies of colliding protons and constitutes around $15\%$ of the leading-order calculation. The influence of the polarization of colliding protons on the next-to-leading-order calculation is more significant than on the leading-order calculation.

### [16] [Emergent Gauge Symmetries in Particle Physics and Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19403)
*Steven D. Bass*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了规范对称性起源的问题，提出标准模型可能是涌现的，其规范对称性在紫外区的某个相变中消失。希格斯真空的（亚）稳定性可能指向极高能标的新临界现象，暗能量尺度与马约拉纳中微子质量在同一量级（约10^16 GeV涌现能标），暗物质候选者包括轴子和涌现能标以上自由度的声子激发，可能的检验涉及中微子和早期宇宙引力波信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索规范对称性的起源，解释标准模型可能并非基本理论，而是在某个更高能标下涌现出来的有效理论，并为希格斯真空稳定性、暗能量尺度与中微子质量关联等未解之谜提供统一视角。

Method: 基于涌现思想，假设标准模型的规范对称性在紫外区某相变中消解；利用低能展开，以涌现能标（约10^16 GeV）的倒数幂次作为小参数，分析暗能量尺度与马约拉纳中微子质量出现在同一阶的自然性。

Result: 暗能量尺度与轻型马约拉纳中微子质量在涌现能标的低能展开中出现在同一量级；提出轴子和涌现能标以上自由度的声子激发作为暗物质候选；预测可通过中微子实验和早期宇宙引力波信号检验该模型。

Conclusion: 标准模型可能是涌现理论，希格斯场连接实验室能标与紫外区新临界现象，暗能量与中微子质量的自然关联支持涌现图像，引力波和中微子是检验该场景的关键探针。

Abstract: Where do gauge symmetries come from? These lectures develop the idea that the Standard Model might be emergent, with its gauge symmetries dissolving in some phase transition deep in the ultraviolet. The (meta-)stability of the Higgs vacuum may be pointing to some new critical phenomena at very high energy scales, with the Higgs connecting physics at LHC laboratory energies to that in the deep ultraviolet. In the emergence scenario, the dark energy scale comes out similar to the size of light Majorana neutrino masses. These two quantities appear at the same order in a low energy expansion in inverse powers of the scale of emergence, about $10^{16}$ GeV. Dark matter candidates include axions and phonon like excitations of degrees of freedom above the scale of emergence. Possible tests of these ideas involve neutrinos as well as gravitational-waves-related signals from the early Universe, which are sensitive to physics at very high energy scales.

### [17] [LeWRON: Agentic Analysis of Electroweak Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19425)
*Isaac R. Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: LeWRON是一个自动化电弱相变分析的智能代理框架，能从输入拉氏量出发，自主完成有效势构建、热历史追踪、气泡成核率计算和引力波谱预测等完整流程，支持复现已有结果和探索新模型两种模式，并通过审计模块确保可重复性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电弱相变分析涉及从有限温度有效势构建到引力波谱预测的复杂流水线，技术门槛高、对约定敏感且模型依赖性强，现有流程缺乏自动化、可复现的端到端工具。

Method: 提出LeWRON代理框架，包含审计工具箱构建模块和Explorer探索模块；通过审计代理检查中间分析输出，存储为结构化工件；支持复现模式（从文献推断约定并复现结果）和发现模式（引导用户通过结构化检查点探索新模型）。

Result: 在多个代表性超越标准模型场景中进行了演示验证，并已在GitHub上开源。

Conclusion: LeWRON成功地将电弱相变分析流水线自动化、模块化，提升了可重复性和易用性，为连接对撞机现象学、重子产生和引力波观测提供了高效工具。

Abstract: The electroweak phase transition (EWPT) is a central topic in particle physics and cosmology, connecting collider phenomenology, baryogenesis, and gravitational-wave observatories. Its analysis requires a technically demanding, convention-sensitive, and model-dependent pipeline, from constructing the finite-temperature effective potential to tracking thermal histories, computing bubble nucleation rates, and predicting gravitational-wave spectra. We present LeWRON (Learning ElectroWeak phase tRansitiON), an agentic framework that orchestrates this pipeline starting from an input Lagrangian. LeWRON combines audited toolbox construction with an Explorer module that uses the generated model-specific code for further analysis, including scans and plots. Intermediate analytic outputs are checked by auditor agents and stored as structured artifacts, enabling reproducible human inspection and downstream use through both a command-line interface and a public Python API. The framework supports a reproduction mode, which infers conventions from the literature and reproduces published results, and a discovery mode, which guides users through structured checkpoints for new models. We demonstrate LeWRON across representative beyond-the-Standard-Model scenarios and release the code on GitHub.

</details>


### [18] [Partial-wave unitarity and long-range interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19432)
*Ryan Plestid,Pablo Quílez Lasanta*

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 含无质量粒子的理论中，t-通道（前向散射）奇点导致标准固定阶微扰论下的分波振幅发散，阻碍了系统可改进的分波幺正性边界的建立。

Method: 在修正的微扰论中研究分波振幅的构造，纳入长程相互作用，重点分析离壳库仑模式的作用，发现前向散射区域存在普适描述，消除了重整化标度依赖。

Result: 得到的改进分波振幅成为定义良好、无伪红外调节器依赖的单尺度对象，并给出了逐阶微扰计算该振幅的实用方法。

Conclusion: 成功解决了前向散射奇点导致的分波振幅发散问题，为构建系统可改进的分波幺正性边界提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Theories with massless particles contain $t$-channel (forward scattering) singularities that cause standard fixed order expressions for partial-wave amplitudes to be ill-defined. This presents an obstruction to systematically improvable partial-wave unitarity bounds. In this work, we study the construction of partial-wave amplitudes in a modified perturbation theory that incorporates long-range interactions focusing on the role of off-shell Coulomb modes. We find that there exists a universal description of the forward scattering region that renders the amplitudes renormalization scale independent. The resulting partial-wave amplitudes become well defined single-scale objects without spurious dependence on the infrared regulator, and we present a practical method for their computation order-by-order in perturbation theory.

### [19] [From Rags to Jeans: Axion Miniclusters from Early matter domination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19439)

Method: 理论上分析了早期物质主导时期辐射浴的不均匀性如何通过轴子质量的温度依赖性诱导空间涨落，进而产生轴子密度扰动的新源项。

Result: 该机制在再加热温度略低于质量饱和尺度T_Λ时最有效，可使轴子超密度达到单位量级；QCD轴子的非线性谱包含两个特征区域，分别对应引力增强和质量温度依赖性效应。

Conclusion: 早期物质主导时期中轴子质量的温度依赖性可有效产生轴子密度扰动，影响极小团块和轴子星的形成，对轴子暗物质结构形成具有重要意义。

Abstract: In an early matter-dominated era, density and temperature inhomogeneities of the radiation bath grow more efficiently than in the standard radiation-dominated history. If the axion mass depends on temperature, these inhomogeneities induce spatial fluctuations of the axion mass, providing a new source term for axion density perturbations. We show that this mechanism is most efficient when the reheating temperature lies just below the mass-saturation scale $T_Λ$, and can drive axion overdensities to order unity by matter--radiation equality. For the QCD axion saturating the observed dark matter abundance, the nonlinear spectrum at equality exhibits two characteristic regions: one associated with the gravitational enhancement already present in moduli-driven cosmologies, and another produced by the temperature dependence of the axion mass. We estimate the resulting minicluster masses and discuss the possible formation of axion miniclusters and axion-star substructure.

Abstract: A variety of experiments are operating or planned to search for displaced decays of light long-lived dark sector particles. In case such a state is discovered, the next step is determining its quantum numbers. We identify an angular observable, reconstructible solely from the decay products' four-momenta, that exhibits an anisotropic distribution for vector bosons from light meson decays and an isotropic distribution for scalars. ### [21] [Real and Virtual Propagation in Neutrino Oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19548)
*Kenji Nishiwaki,Kin-ya Oda,Juntaro Wada*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了真空中味振荡的传播时间依赖性，通过鞍点法推导出味改变振幅的扩展表达式，发现振荡仅在传播时间超过由外部波包能量不确定性和传播粒子衰变宽度设定的阈值时发生，短传播时间内中间粒子表现为纯虚态，无法宏观传播。该结果意味着 Jacob-Sachs 定理在短传播时间下比预期更精确。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重新审视真空中味振荡的传播时间依赖性，澄清短传播时间下中间态的行为，特别是从虚态到实态传播的转变条件。

Method: 采用波包量子场论框架，利用鞍点法显式评估相关积分，推导出味改变振幅的扩展表达式，该表达式在短传播时间下仍然有效。

Result: 振荡仅当传播时间超过由外部波包能量不确定性和传播粒子衰变宽度设定的阈值时才发生；短传播时间内中间粒子表现为纯虚态，无法宏观距离传播；Jacob-Sachs 定理在短传播时间下比预期更精确。

Conclusion: 该形式不仅适用于中微子，也适用于其他传播粒子；未来能量分辨率的提升可能使该阈值变得可观测；直接实验检验从虚到实传播的转变具有挑战性，因其通常发生在微观尺度。

Abstract: We revisit flavor oscillations in vacuum in terms of the propagation time of intermediate states. In the limit of a long propagation time (or distance), degenerate intermediate states exhibit oscillatory behavior, as described by the Jacob--Sachs (or Grimus--Stockinger) theorem within wave-packet quantum field theory. By explicitly evaluating the relevant integrals using the saddle-point method, we derive an extended expression for the flavor-changing amplitude that remains valid even for shorter propagation times. We show that oscillations occur only when the propagation time exceeds a threshold set by the energy uncertainty of the external wave packets and by the decay width of the propagating particle. For shorter propagation, the intermediate particle behaves as a purely virtual state, in the sense that it cannot propagate over a macroscopic distance. Although a direct experimental test of the transition from virtual to real propagation is challenging, since it typically occurs at microscopic scales, our result implies that the Jacob--Sachs theorem holds to higher accuracy than previously expected, even at short propagation times. Our formalism applies not only to neutrinos but also to other propagating particles, and future improvements in energy resolution may make this threshold observable.

</details>


### [22] [Freeze-in at all couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19564)
*Andreas Goudelis,Andre Lessa,Lucas Magno Dantas Ramos,Thomas Reggio*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文分析了带电母体冻入暗物质模型，重点研究宇宙再加热温度低于或等于理论质量标度的情形。在此配置下，暗物质产生受玻尔兹曼抑制，允许更强的耦合但仍能重现观测丰度。研究表明，追踪暗物质和中介子的数密度演化对于获得可靠预测至关重要，包括中介子因快速衰变而无法热化的意外行为。最后，更新了LHC搜索和轻子味 violating 衰变的约束，展示了这些搜索在探测宇宙学可行参数空间中的互补性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究宇宙再加热温度较低（与理论质量标度相当或更低）时，带电母体冻入暗物质模型的行为，因为此区域暗物质产生受玻尔兹曼抑制，可允许更强的暗物质-标准模型耦合，从而扩大模型的可探测参数空间。

Method: 采用带电母体冻入（parent freeze-in）暗物质模型，通过求解暗物质与中介子的数密度演化方程，分析再加热温度、中介子与暗物质质量、耦合强度之间的非平凡相互作用。同时结合LHC搜索和轻子味 violating 衰变等实验约束。

Result: 发现追踪暗物质和中介子的数密度演化是必要的，且观察到中介子因快速衰变而无法热化的意外行为。更新了来自LHC搜索和轻子味 violating 衰变的实验约束，并展示了这些搜索在探测宇宙学可行参数空间中的互补性。

Conclusion: 在低再加热温度场景下，带电母体冻入机制是可行的暗物质产生途径，但需要仔细处理数密度演化以获得可靠预测，且多种实验搜索在约束参数空间方面具有互补作用。

Abstract: We perform a comprehensive analysis of a charged parent freeze-in dark matter model, focusing on scenarios where the Universe reheats to a temperature comparable to or lower than the mass scales of the theory. In such configurations, dark matter production is Boltzmann-suppressed, allowing for stronger couplings between dark matter and the Standard Model thermal bath while still reproducing the observed relic abundance. We emphasize the non-trivial interplay between the reheating temperature, the mediator and dark matter masses and the coupling strength. We show that tracking the number density evolution of both dark matter and the mediator is essential to obtain reliable predictions, including unexpected behaviors such as the mediator non-equilibration due to fast decays. Lastly, we explore the phenomenological implications of this scenario, updating constraints from LHC searches and lepton flavour-violating decays and highlighting the complementarity of these searches in probing the cosmologically viable parameter space.

Conclusion: 该过程对质子半径尺度具有非平凡的敏感性，但当前结果尚不足以最终解决质子半径之谜，需要更多精确数据。

Abstract: We study the exclusive production of dileptons in proton--proton collisions as a probe of the proton radius. Using a dipole form factor model, we compare the conventional choice of $Λ^2=0.71$~GeV$^2$ with PDG test scenarios corresponding to $r_p=0.8751$~fm and $r_p=0.84087$~fm. ### [24] [$U(1)_{B-L}$ Dark Matter Constrains Smooth (SUSY) Hybrid Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19612)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 暗物质 relic丰度观测值对暴胀参数空间产生强约束，标量谱指数被限制在n_s ≃ 0.972-0.974的狭窄区间。暴胀子-暗物质耦合对背景演化影响可忽略，但会显著改变张标比r和原初引力波谱。

Conclusion: 建立了暴胀与暗物质产生间的直接理论联系，表明暗物质物理可以反过来约束暴胀模型参数，并通过引力波观测检验该框架。n_s的高度预测性为未来宇宙学观测提供了可检验信号。

Abstract: We propose a unified framework that connects inflationary dynamics with dark matter production within a supersymmetric $U(1)_{B-L}$ extension of the Standard Model. The setup is based on smooth hybrid inflation embedded in supergravity, with a non-minimal Kahler potential ensuring control of higher-order corrections. The model involves three scalar fields: the inflaton $σ$, an auxiliary field $ζ$ responsible for ending inflation, and a singlet mediator $η$ that links the inflationary and dark sectors. Dark matter is realized as an inert scalar stabilized by a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry and produced non-thermally via reheating dynamics. We show that reproducing the observed dark matter relic abundance imposes strong constraints on the inflationary sector, significantly reducing the allowed parameter space. As a result, the scalar spectral index is tightly constrained to $n_s \simeq 0.972 - 0.974$, consistent with current observational bounds. While the inflaton-dark matter coupling has a negligible effect on the background evolution, it induces observable modifications in the tensor-to-scalar ratio and the spectrum of primordial gravitational waves. This establishes a direct link between dark matter physics and inflationary observables.

We compare our sensitivities with those from low-energy CLFV searches, as well as from current and future collider experiments. ### [26] [Constraining ADD black holes at the LHC with $\sqrt{s} = 14$ TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19839)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于ADD模型，在$\sqrt{s}=14~\mathrm{TeV}$、积分亮度$349.4~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$的条件下，引入参数$\zeta$表征黑洞形成过程中的能量损失，分析不同额外维度数$\mathcal{D}$和约化普朗克标度$\Lambda_{\mathcal{D}}$下的黑洞质量$M_{\mathrm{B}}$排除限。

Conclusion: 能量损失效应显著降低了黑洞质量的下限约束；额外维度数目越多，约束越强；研究为LHC上微观黑洞的搜寻提供了更精确的理论参考。

Abstract: We explore microscopic black holes at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) in the context of the ADD model for the centre-of-mass energy $\sqrt{s} = 14~\mathrm{TeV}$ at an integrated luminosity of $349.4~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ and provide constraints on the black hole mass, $M_{\mathrm{B}}$ by taking into account the effects of loss during the formation process of black holes through the parameter $ζ$. Our analysis reveals that for $ζ= 0$, black holes with $M_{\mathrm{B}} \leq 11.83~\mathrm{TeV}$ are disfavored in the case of three extra dimensions ($\mathcal{D}$), for the reduced Planck scale ($Λ_{\mathcal{D}}$) of about a TeV. The corresponding values for $Λ_{\mathcal{D}} = 9~\mathrm{TeV}$ turned out to be about $10.33~\mathrm{TeV}$. A significant reduction in the aforementioned limits is observed while the loss gets higher, e.g. for $ζ= 0.35$, $M_{\mathrm{B}}$ reduces to $7.65 (6.82)~\mathrm{TeV}$ at $Λ_{\mathcal{D}} = 1 (9)~\mathrm{TeV}$. These limits change to $12.03 ~(10.88)~\mathrm{TeV}$ and $7.80~ (7.03)~\mathrm{TeV}$ respectively for $ζ= 0~(0.35)$ for $Λ_{\mathcal{D}} = 1 (9)~\mathrm{TeV}$ at 95\% C.L. in case $\mathcal{D}$ is raised to seven.

Abstract: We assess the tension between theoretical predictions and the values quoted by the Particle Data Group (PDG) for the partial decay width and branching fraction associated with the radiative charmonium decay $J/ψ\toγη_c$. This approach obviates the need to modify the photon energy spectrum line shape using empirical damping functions, as done in the most recent experimental extractions of $\mathcal{B}(J/ψ\toγη_c)$ from the photon line shape, thereby eliminating an inherent ambiguity in the determination of the derived observables.

### [28] [New Avenues of Heavy Neutral Lepton at Muon Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19906)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 本文提出的$Z'Z'$融合过程为在多TeV缪子对撞机上探测重中性轻子$N$提供了替代且有效的新途径，有助于揭示重中性轻子的内在特征，拓展了现有搜索策略的覆盖范围。

Abstract: With initial state radiation, the multi-TeV muon collider can be regarded as an electroweak boson collider. The dominant production mode of the certain process becomes the vector boson fusion channel, because the corresponding cross section typically increases logarithmically at high energies. This also holds true for new physics beyond the standard model. Within the $U(1)$ gauged extension of seesaw models, the heavy neutral lepton has additional interactions with the new gauge boson $Z'$ and heavy Higgs $H$. In this paper, we investigate the production of heavy neutral lepton $N$ via the new vector boson fusion processes $Z'Z'\to H\to NN$ with and $Z'Z'\to NN$ without heavy Higgs at the multi-TeV muon collider. Different from the canonical vector boson fusion processes $WW/ZZ\to H\to NN$, the new process $Z'Z'\to H\to NN$ is not suppressed by the small mixing angle $α$ between the Higgs bosons. Meanwhile, the pair production process $Z'Z'\to NN$ is also viable even for heavy Higgs $m_H> \sqrt{s}$. Therefore, these new avenues provide alternative pathways to probe the intrinsic feature of the heavy neutral lepton. We then perform a detailed analysis of the lepton number violation signals via the new vector boson fusion with heavy Higgs $μ^+μ^-\to μ^+μ^- H \to μ^+μ^- NN$ and without heavy Higgs $μ^+μ^-\to μ^+μ^- NN$, followed by $N\to μ^\pm jj$, where the two jets from $W$ boson decay are treated as one fat-jet $J$.

Abstract: The recent LHCb observation of $Ξ_{cc}^{+}$ opens the ultra-low-$Q$ transition $Ξ_{cc}^{++}\toΞ_{cc}^{+}$ as an experimentally motivated null test of charged-current new physics. Our two- and three-body analyses show sensitivity to effective baryon-level couplings of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-6}-10^{-7})$ for MeV-scale recoil momenta. We establish a practical no-go result for a universal light charged scalar $φ^+$: with a first-generation $φ^+\bar u d$ coupling, existing electroweak-precision and beta-decay constraints are parametrically stronger than the projected LHCb sensitivity. We then identify a two-charm-selective charged-current portal whose leading operator has a nonzero matrix element in doubly charmed baryons but vanishes at leading order in pions, nucleons, nuclei, and singly charmed mesons. In this class of models, $Ξ_{cc}^{++}\toΞ_{cc}^{+}$ transitions can provide the leading direct probe of the portal interaction.

Abstract: Vector-boson scattering with semileptonic final states has recently been measured at the LHC, and future experiments are expected to further increase the precision of its measurement, calling for adequate theoretical predictions. In this work, we present a calculation of the NLO QCD and electroweak corrections to the process $\text{p}\text{p} \to \ell^+ ν_\ell + 4\text{j}$ in two different fiducial regions relevant for vector-boson scattering. In a fully off-shell calculation, we provide results for the leading electroweak contribution of $\mathcal{O}\left(α^6\right)$ and the corresponding corrections of $\mathcal{O}\left(α^7\right)$ and $\mathcal{O}\left(α_\text{s} α^6\right)$ for fiducial cross sections and a selection of differential distributions.

### [31] [Two Flavon Froggatt-Nielsen Models with Genetic Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20000)

Method: 将寻找唯象可行模型转化为多目标优化问题，每个实验约束作为独立目标；使用非支配排序遗传算法 III（NSGA-III）同时拟合 18 个 FN 电荷、45 个 Wilson 系数以及 flavon 参数，覆盖夸克和轻子扇区。

Abstract: We present the first systematic and comprehensive scan of two-flavon Froggatt-Nielsen (FN) models, employing artificial intelligence techniques to explore the high-dimensional, mixed discrete-continuous parameter space. Extending the standard single-flavon FN framework to a two-flavon setup in which separate flavon fields couple independently to the up- and down-type sectors, we demonstrate that the relative phase between their vacuum expectation values (vevs) provides a natural and generic source of CP violation absent in single-flavon models. To explore this enlarged model space, we cast the search for phenomenologically viable models as a multi-objective optimisation problem, formulating each experimental constraint as a separate objective, and employ the Non-dominated Sorting Genetic Algorithm III to simultaneously fit all 18 FN charges, 45 Wilson coefficients, and flavon parameters to both the quark and lepton sectors. Our approach requires no separate training phase and identifies phenomenologically viable models orders of magnitude faster than prior reinforcement learning methods. The expected discovery sensitivity is evaluated using the Asimov significance for an integrated luminosity of $3$ ab$^{-1}$ at $\sqrt{s}=14$ TeV. Our results demonstrate that the $2τ\:+\:2b\:+$ missing $E_T$ channel provides a promising and largely orthogonal avenue to search for non-standard VLQ decays in extended Higgs sectors, with discovery-level sensitivity achievable for VLQ masses up to approximately $1.9$ TeV.

*Sin Kyu Kang,Ranjeet Kumar,Hemant Kumar Prajapati*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于反常自由 $U(1)_{B-L}$ 电荷分配 $(-4,-4,5)$ 的狄拉克中微子跷跷板-跷跷板框架，其中大气中微子质量平方差在树图级别产生，太阳中微子质量平方差通过辐射修正产生，自发对称性破缺后残余 $Z_6$ 对称性稳定暗物质候选者，探索了两种最小实现并分析了暗物质现象学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在标准模型中，中微子质量和暗物质的存在缺乏自然解释。现有 $U(1)_{B-L}$ 模型通常采用矢量型电荷分配，难以同时解释中微子质量谱的层次结构和暗物质稳定性。本文旨在通过一个反常自由的 chiral $U(1)_{B-L}$ 框架，统一解释中微子质量、暗物质稳定性及相关实验约束。

Method: 采用 Dirac scoto-seesaw 机制，对右手中微子赋予反常自由 chiral 电荷 $(-4,-4,5)$；大气中微子质量差通过树图 seesaw 产生，太阳中微子质量差通过单圈辐射修正产生；$U(1)_{B-L}$ 自发破缺后残余 $Z_6$ 对称性自然稳定暗物质；分析两种最小实现（分别对应不同粒子内容）中的中微子质量序（NO/IO）可行性；研究标量单态和费米子单态两种暗物质候选者的现象学，包括 $Z'$ 门户、湮灭和共湮灭通道。

Result: 两种最小实现中，一种允许正常序和倒转序均可行，另一种仅允许正常序存活；Chiral 电荷分配抑制了 $Z'$ 的双轻子衰变分支比，导致 ATLAS 给出的质量约束弱于常规矢量 $B-L$ 模型，从而放宽了对暗物质区域的限制；标量单态暗物质通常受到强约束，但 $Z'$ 门户结合湮灭和共湮灭通道显著拓宽了允许的参数空间。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一个可预测的中微子和暗物质现象学方案，能够同时在正常序和倒转序（取决于具体实现）下解释观测到的中微子质量平方差，并通过残余对称性自然稳定暗物质，其独特的 $Z'$ 信号特征可在未来实验中被检验。

Abstract: We present a simple Dirac scoto-seesaw framework based on the anomaly-free $U(1)_{B-L}$ charge assignment $(-4,-4,5)$ for $ν_R$. This chiral charge assignment naturally accounts for the observed neutrino mass-squared differences, with $Δm^2_{\rm atm}$ generated at tree level and $Δm^2_{\rm sol}$ arising radiatively. After the spontaneous breaking of gauged $U(1)_{B-L}$, a residual $Z_6$ symmetry stabilizes the dark matter candidate. We investigate two minimal realizations of the framework, finding that both normal and inverted orderings are viable in one case, whereas only normal ordering survives in the other, with distinctive features for neutrino observables. Moreover, the chiral nature of the $U(1)_{B-L}$ charges suppresses the dilepton branching fraction of $Z'$, resulting in weaker ATLAS mass bounds than in the conventional vector $B-L$ scenario, thereby easing constraints on the dark sector. We explore the dark matter phenomenology of the singlet scalar and fermionic dark matter candidates. While singlet scalar DM is often severely constrained, the presence of the $Z'$ portal together with annihilation and co-annihilation channels substantially broadens the allowed parameter space. Thus, the framework offers a predictive scenario for neutrino and dark matter phenomenology that can be probed in future experiments.

Abstract: We present a systematic study of the three-particle di-light-cone distribution amplitudes (DLCDAs) of the $B$-meson. They are defined through $B$-meson--to--vacuum matrix elements of trilocal HQET operators, in which the light antiquark and the gluon field-strength tensor are located on two back-to-back light rays. In this sense, the DLCDAs generalise the conventional $B$-meson light-cone distribution amplitudes to configurations where soft fields couple to collinear degrees of freedom in two distinct directions. As such, they parametrise the non-perturbative dynamics associated with non-factorisable soft-gluon contributions in rare and non-leptonic exclusive $B$-meson decays. We derive the complete Lorentz decomposition of the matrix elements of generic trilocal operators, identify eight independent DLCDAs, and organise them in a basis of definite twist. Using local operator identities and equations-of-motion constraints, we obtain tree-level relations for their normalisation integrals and first moments in terms of a minimal set of hadronic parameters. These relations allow us to construct simple momentum-space models for all independent DLCDAs. For the leading-twist distribution, we further incorporate the perturbative radiative tail at order $α_s$ and discuss its impact on the resulting parametrisation.

Motivation: 探索弦理论中大量轻轴子物种（弦轴子景）通过原初黑洞的霍金蒸發和超辐射过程对暗物质产生的影响，以及这些轴子对暗物质构成和宇宙学观测的潜在可观测效应。

Method: 理论分析原初黑洞通过霍金蒸發发射大量轴子物种的过程，以及这些轴子物种对超辐射效率的影响，进而计算原初黑洞自旋变化、超辐射云增长以及最终暗物质组分（如微玻色子星）的形成条件；同时评估蒸發轴子对有效中微子自由度（Neff）的贡献。

Result: 弦轴子景（约100-10^5种轻轴子）可显著增强超辐射效率，扩大暗物质以微玻色子星形式存在的参数空间（暗物质质量、PBH质量和自旋）；但轴子物种过多时PBH蒸發过快，超辐射云无法达到最大质量；蒸發产生的轴子对Neff贡献极小，不可观测。

Conclusion: 弦理论预测的大量轻轴子物种通过原初黑洞的超辐射过程可显著改变暗物质产生机制，扩大了微玻色子星作为暗物质候选者的可能性，但轴子物种数量存在上限约束；蒸發轴子对宇宙学观测（如Neff）无显著影响。

Abstract: We study the effects of string axion emission on dark matter production by light primordial black holes (PBHs), through both evaporation and superradiance. We show, in particular, that the Hawking emission of $\mathcal{O}(100-10^5)$ light axion species predicted in realistic string theory constructions can significantly enhance the efficiency of superradiance, given the associated increase in the PBH spin. The string axiverse thus significantly expands the parametric regions (dark matter mass and PBH mass and spin) for which a sizeable fraction of dark matter may presently be in the form of ``micro-boson stars'': the self-gravitating remnants of superradiant dark matter clouds. Conversely, for too large a number of axion species PBHs evaporate too quickly for superradiant clouds to attain their maximum mass. Finally, assuming that all dark matter is produced by PBHs (through both superradiance and Hawking emission), we show that the axions emitted during PBH evaporation give an immeasurably small contribution to the relativistic degrees of freedom at recombination.

</details>

Abstract: We investigate the implications of the Witten effect in the Standard Model with a general global gauge group structure and determine the values of the three $θ$-parameters that lead to distinct families of allowed spectra of dyons. We construct and classify the corresponding dyonic charge lattices consistent with the Standard Model gauge structure. This approach enables us to re-derive the known global-group--dependent periodicities of the $θ$ angles and to determine all CP-invariant points in $θ$-space. The electromagnetic subgroup $U(1)_{\mathrm{em}}$ is shown to arise \emph{prior} to electroweak symmetry breaking by factoring out the effect of the anomalous $B+L$ transformations, which reduces the physical $θ$-parameter space from a three-torus to a two-torus. Our phenomenological conclusions include an observation that a discovery of a $U(1)_{\mathrm{em}}$ monopole carrying non-zero electric charge would determine the last remaining unknown parameter of the Standard Model. Lastly we study how $θ$-space shapes axion physics with emphasis on the axion-photon coupling and show that a single axion is insufficient to render the Standard Model vacuum fully CP invariant.

### [43] [New Gauge Forces, Neutron Stars and Schwinger Neutrino Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20393)
*Yuxin Liu,Zhen Liu,Andrey Shkerin,Jing Shu,Yue Zhao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究B-L、L_e-L_{μ/τ}或L_μ-L_τ规范对称性引起的新长程力对中微子的影响。天体产生的轻子势会导致带电中微子的Schwinger对产生，形成简并费米气体或稳定中微子通量。对于B-L和L_e-L_{μ/τ}力，效应太弱不可观测；对于L_μ-L_τ力，当中微子耦合常数g≳10^{-18}时在中子星中显著，会改变元素丰度并压制电荷，使中子星合并的约束失效。该中微子通量可能被距离约100 pc的年轻中子星探测到，典型能量约100 MeV，专门搜索可重新确立g≲10^{-18}的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超出标准模型的新长程力（源于B-L、L_e-L_{μ/τ}或L_μ-L_τ规范对称性）对中微子的影响，并研究这些效应在天体物理环境中的可观测性。

Method: 分析天体（地球、太阳、中子星）产生的轻子势导致带电中微子的Schwinger对产生机制，研究对产生粒子的动力学行为（简并费米气体形成与稳态通量），并评估不同规范对称性及耦合强度下的可观测性。

Result: B-L和L_e-L_{μ/τ}力效应太弱不可观测；L_μ-L_τ力在中子星中耦合常数g≳10^{-18}时效应显著，会改变元素丰度并压制L_μ-L_τ电荷，使现有中子星合并约束失效；该Schwinger效应产生的~100 MeV中微子通量可能被~100 pc内的年轻中子星探测到。

Conclusion: L_μ-L_τ长程力在中子星中产生可观测效应，专门搜寻该中微子信号可将耦合常数约束重新确立为g≲10^{-18}。

Abstract: We investigate neutrino effects of new long-range forces arising from gauging $B-L$, $L_e-L_{μ/τ}$ or $L_μ-L_τ$ symmetries of the Standard Model. The leptonic potential generated by astronomical bodies, such as the Earth, the Sun or a neutron star, results in the Schwinger pair production of neutrinos charged under the new gauge symmetry. The oppositely charged particles accumulate in the potential well forming a degenerate Fermi gas, while equally charged particles fly away forming a steady flux of neutrinos. We find that, for the $B-L$ and $L_e-L_{μ/τ}$ forces, these effects are too weak to be observable. For the $L_μ-L_τ$ force these effects are significant in neutron stars if the gauge coupling is $g\gtrsim 10^{-18}$. The muonic force changes the element abundances of a neutron star in equilibrium and suppresses its $L_μ-L_τ$ charge. This invalidates the constraint on $g$ from neutron star mergers, at $g\gtrsim 10^{-17}$. Furthermore, for such values of $g$, the neutrino flux produced by the Schwinger effect could potentially be detected from a single young neutron star at a distance of $\simeq 100$ pc, with the typical neutrino energy $E_ν\sim 100$ MeV. A dedicated search for such a signal will reassert the bound $g\lesssim 10^{-18}$.

### [45] [The $B^+ \to K^+ ν\bar ν$ decay as a QCD axion search: comparing reinterpretation approaches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20525)
*Merna Abumusabh,Giulio Dujany,Diego Guadagnoli,Méril Reboud,Claudio Toni*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文追溯了Belle II $B^+ \to K^+ν\barν$数据对$B^+ \to K^+ a$衰变分支比限定的四倍差异，发现根源在于运动学变量空间的选择。基于重建双中微子不变质量$q^2_{\rm rec}$的精细分箱能有效分辨窄宽度轴子信号，而粗分箱或BDT变量空间会稀释信号。作者主张实验合作在发布BDT似然的同时发布物理变量空间的似然投影，以最大化测量的可重解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释Belle II $B^+ \to K^+ν\barν$数据对$B^+ \to K^+ a$分支比限定的四倍差异来源，并评估不同分析策略的有效性和保守性。

Method: 对比不同运动学变量空间（$q^2_{\rm rec}$精细/粗分箱、$q^2_{\rm rec} \times \eta({\rm BDT}_2)$空间）下的统计敏感性；通过数值测试验证BDT变量与$q^2$的低相关性；分析亚领头形状系统误差的影响。

Result: 四倍灵敏度差异完全由运动学轴选择导致；$q^2_{\rm rec}$精细分箱法对轴子信号最灵敏且结果是保守的（形状系统误差只会进一步降低上限）；BDT变量与$q^2$几乎不相关，无法有效区分$B^+ \to K^+ a$与$B^+ \to K^+ν\barν$。

Conclusion: 基于BDT的似然在信号形状与训练信号差异大时可重解释性有限，建议实验合作同时发布物理变量空间上的似然投影以增强测量结果的复用性。

Abstract: Two recent independent analyses of Belle II $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$ data yield limits on ${\mathcal B}(B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a)$ -- the two-body mode to a light invisible particle such as the QCD axion -- differing by a factor of roughly four; we trace this to the choice of kinematic variable space. The central figure of merit is the resolution in the reconstructed di-neutrino invariant mass $q^2_{\rm rec}$: fine-grained binning resolves the narrow axion signal, while coarse binning dilutes it into a background-dominated range. A BDT axis trained on $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$ adds little discriminating power for $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$, as this axis is largely uncorrelated with $q^2$. These expectations are confirmed by a set of numerical tests. The subleading shape systematics omitted from our $q^2_{\rm rec}$-based approach {\em lower}, not raise, the $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$ limit: by better accommodating the $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$ shape, they leave less room for the axion signal, making our $q^2_{\rm rec}$-based bound conservative, if anything. A dedicated reanalysis confirms that the kinematic-axes choice alone accounts for the factor-of-four sensitivity difference, and that the $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$ bound varies sizeably within the $q^2_{\rm rec}\timesη({\rm BDT}_2)$ space, depending on the SM-likeness of $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$, thus losing the dual-probe feature of our $q^2_{\rm rec}$-based approach. These results point to a broader consideration: likelihoods dominated by BDT variables are of limited use for reinterpretations when the signal shape differs appreciably from the BDT's training signal. We therefore advocate that experimental collaborations publish likelihood projections in physical variable spaces alongside BDT-based likelihoods, to maximise the reinterpretability of their measurements.

Method: 利用弛豫时间近似下的玻尔兹曼输运方程，在避开π⁺凝聚参数区域内计算纵向电导率、热导率和塞贝克系数。

Result: 磁场抑制而旋转增强输运系数；旋转超过一定角速度后可逆转为磁场增强；π⁺在特定参数下凝聚而π⁻不凝聚。

Conclusion: 旋转作为有效化学势引入能量偏移，可超越磁场的抑制作用，显著改变磁化π介子介质的输运特性。

Abstract: This work investigates the electric, thermal, and thermoelectric responses of a rotating pion gas of finite transverse radius in the presence of a background magnetic field, with the rotation axis aligned with the magnetic field. We explicitly calculate the parameter limits for $π^+$ condensation and restrict our working regime safely outside these boundaries, ensuring well-behaved transport coefficients. Notably, the system exhibits a condensation asymmetry, with $π^-$ remaining uncondensed at the parameters that induce $π^+$ condensation. Using the Boltzmann Transport Equation under the Relaxation Time Approximation, we calculate the longitudinal electrical conductivity, thermal conductivity, and the Seebeck coefficient. Our results reveal a competing interplay between the magnetic field and rotation, highlighting the substantial impact of rotation on the medium's transport properties: while the magnetic field suppresses the transport coefficients in a static medium, rotation, acting as an effective chemical potential, introduces an energy shift that favors their increase. Beyond an angular velocity, this rotational enhancement overpowers the magnetic suppression, leading to an increase in the transport coefficients with increasing magnetic field. Finally, we analyze the relative significance of charge and heat transport through the Lorenz number, providing further insight into the transport characteristics of the rotating magnetized pion medium.

</details>

### [47] [Universal Properties of Nonlinearly Perturbed Maxwell Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19845)
*Tengyang Liu,Yisong Yang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了一类广义非线性扰动麦克斯韦电磁理论具有三个普适基本性质：有限能量的点电荷、排除有限能量的磁单极子和双荷子、点电荷有效半径可任意小及相应的局域不可探测性，为电子作为点电荷的不可见性提供了经典解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究非线性扰动下的麦克斯韦理论是否能够保持某些普适的物理性质，特别是为电子作为点电荷的不可见性提供经典层面的理论解释。

Method: 在麦克斯韦理论中引入尽可能一般的非线性扰动轮廓，构建最小扰动模型，并证明该模型下三个普适性质（有限能量点电荷、排除磁单极子和双荷子、有效半径任意小）同时成立。

Result: 该非线性电磁理论成功保持了三个普适性质：点电荷具有有限能量；磁单极子和双荷子被排除（无有限能量解）；点电荷的有效半径可以任意小，从而在经典层面解释了电子的不可见性。

Conclusion: 该非线性理论以最小方式扰动麦克斯韦理论，同时维持了三个关键的普适性质，为理解点电荷（如电子）的经典行为提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We show that a general nonlinearly perturbed Maxwell theory of electromagnetism possesses three universal fundamental properties:
  (i) A finite-energy electric point charge.
  (ii) Exclusion of finite-energy magnetic monopoles and dually charged dyons.
  (iii) Arbitrary smallness of the effective radius of a point electric charge and the associated local undetectedness of the electric charge and energy.
  In particular, this last property offers a classical explanation for the invisibility of the electron, as a point electric charge, in accordance with the smallness of its effective radius.
  This nonlinear theory of electromagnetism has the feature that it minimally perturbs the Maxwell theory with a nonlinearity profile that is as general as possible such that the three universal properties stated above are all maintained.

### [48] [Dirac structures on tangent bundles: a geometric framework for variational principles, constrained dynamics, and symmetry reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20012)
*Hiroaki Yoshimura*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种由拉格朗日二形式和约束分布自然诱导的切丛上的狄拉克结构（拉格朗日-狄拉克结构），为包含非完整、退化拉格朗日及对称系统的拉格朗日-狄拉克动力学系统提供了统一几何框架。该结构具有规范协变性，并衍生出切丛上的变分原理（拉格朗日-达朗贝尔-狄拉克原理）、李群对称性约化理论（欧拉-庞加莱-狄拉克方程）以及无限维扩展（理想流体欧拉方程）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的非完整力学、退化拉格朗日系统和对称系统的几何描述缺乏一个统一的框架。传统拉格朗日力学在处理非完整约束或退化拉格朗日量时面临困难，而狄拉克结构在哈密顿力学中已有成功应用，将其拓展到拉格朗日体系并纳入约束分布是自然且必要的。

Method: 利用拉格朗日二形式和约束分布在切丛上构造拉格朗日-狄拉克结构；引入规范变换概念描述非完整动力学中拉格朗日二形式的不变性；提出切丛上的内在变分原理（拉格朗日-达朗贝尔-狄拉克原理）；利用李群对称性发展约化理论，导出约化后的狄拉克结构和约化变分原理。

Result: 建立了统一的拉格朗日-狄拉克结构几何框架；揭示了非完整动力学的规范协变性；得到了超正则情形下的拉格朗日-达朗贝尔方程的一阶形式；导出了约化后的欧拉-庞加莱-狄拉克方程；成功应用于带电粒子、电路、速度线性拉格朗日系统及理想流体等示例。

Conclusion: 拉格朗日-狄拉克结构为约束力学系统提供了一个统一、内在的几何描述，包含了非完整约束、退化拉格朗日量、对称性约化等多种情形。该框架具有自然的规范协变性，并能推广到无限维情形（如流体力学），在几何力学和数学物理中具有重要的理论价值和广泛应用前景。

Abstract: We introduce a Dirac structure on the tangent bundle of a configuration manifold, called a \textit{Lagrange--Dirac structure}, which is naturally induced by the Lagrangian two-form associated with a (possibly degenerate) Lagrangian and a constraint distribution. This structure provides a unified geometric framework for Lagrange--Dirac dynamical systems, encompassing nonholonomic, degenerate Lagrangian, and symmetric systems. In the hyperregular case, the system recovers a first-order formulation of the Lagrange--d'Alembert equations. Although nonholonomic dynamics does not preserve the Lagrangian two-form, we show that the underlying Lagrange--Dirac structure is preserved up to gauge transformations, yielding a natural gauge covariance property.
  We also formulate an intrinsic variational principle directly on the tangent bundle, referred to as the \textit{Lagrange--d'Alembert--Dirac principle}, which recovers Hamilton's principle in the unconstrained case and the Lagrange--d'Alembert principle in the hyperregular constrained case. Furthermore, we develop a reduction theory for systems with Lie group symmetry, deriving a reduced Lagrange--Dirac structure over the Lie algebra that yields the Euler--Poincaré--Dirac equations and a corresponding reduced variational principle. Finally, we illustrate the theory through examples including charged particles, electric circuits, and systems with Lagrangians linear in velocity, and present an infinite-dimensional extension to ideal fluids that naturally incorporates the incompressibility constraint and recovers the Euler equations.

</details>

Method: 通过分析随机薛定谔算子 H = -Δ + ε Σ ω_n χ_n - V 的谱结构，将安德森局域化与吸引势的束缚效应相结合，建立负特征值数量的定量估计。

Our primary focus is to establish precise estimates on the number of negative eigenvalues (bound states) induced by the attractive perturbation. By analyzing the competition between Anderson localization and the binding capacity of the potential, we provide quantitative bounds on the discrete spectrum. These results offer new insights into how randomness enhances the eigenvalue bounds.

### [50] [Fourier-Helgason transform as infinite geodesic time limit in geometric quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20290)
*Ana Cristina Ferreira,Joachim Hilgert,José M. Mourão,João P. Nunes*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 本文解决了非紧对称空间$G/K$上Fourier-Helgason变换与几何量子化之间的不一致性问题。通过将水平极化视为测地流下垂直极化的无穷时间极限，并构造量子测地变换（QGT），证明了该变换在测地时间趋于无穷时的极限与Fourier-Helgason变换相等（相差Harish-Chandra $c$函数的相位和一个无关常数）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lisiecki (1987) 对复Lie群$G$给出了FH变换的几何量子化解释，但对于非复Lie群，BKS配对与FH变换不等价且非酉。本文旨在解决这一不一致性，即对非复Lie群的情况给出FH变换的几何量子化解释。

Method: 1. 证明水平极化是$G$-不变黎曼度量测地流下垂直极化的无穷时间极限；2. 将测地流提升为量子丛上的酉平行输运（量子测地变换QGT）；3. 证明QGT在测地时间趋于无穷时存在极限，并证明该极限等于FH变换（相差Harish-Chandra $c$函数的相位和无关常数）。

Result: 对于非复Lie群$G$，构造的量子测地变换的无穷时间极限与Fourier-Helgason变换相等（相差Harish-Chandra $c$函数的相位和无关常数），从而解决了此前的不一致性。

Conclusion: 本文通过量子测地变换为FH变换提供了统一的几何量子化解释，适用于所有非紧对称空间，不再局限于复Lie群情形。

Abstract: The Fourier-Helgason (FH) transform for a noncompact symmetric space $G/K$ establishes the direct integral decomposition of the unitary representation of $G$ on $L^2(G/K)$ into irreducible principal series representations.
  By applying techniques of geometric quantization to the symplectic manifold $T^*(G/K),$ Lisiecki in 1987 gave a geometric interpretation of the FH transform in the case when $G$ is complex. He defined for general $G$ a ''horizontal'' polarization on $T^*(G/K)$ and showed that, for complex $G$, the Blattner-Kostant-Sternberg (BKS) pairing between the Schrödinger vertical polarization Hilbert space, $L^2(G/K)$, and the Hilbert space of horizontally polarized functions coincides with the FH transform. However, in the same paper, Lisiecki showed that for noncomplex Lie groups the BKS pairing is nonequivalent to the FH transform and nonunitary in general.
  In the present paper, we resolve this discrepancy between the FH transform and geometric quantization in the case when $G$ is not complex.
  First, we show that the horizontal polarization is the infinite-time limit of the push-forward of the vertical polarization with respect to the geodesic flow for a $G$-invariant Riemannian metric. Then we lift the geodesic flow to an intertwining unitary parallel transport on the quantum bundle that we call quantum geodesic transform (QGT). Finally we show that the QGT has a well-defined limit, as the geodesic time goes to infinity, and that it is equal, up to the phase of the Harish-Chandra $c$-function and an irrelevant multiplicative constant, to the FH transform.

</details>

### [51] [Geometric Rigidity via Harmonic Twisted Spinors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19567)
*Francesco Bei,Simone Cecchini*

Main category: math.DG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在标量曲率几何中，研究Gromov提出的精确提升闭双形式方法，建立标量曲率与万有覆盖Laplace谱下确界之间的尖锐比较，并刻画等式成立时的刚性结构。

Method: 利用Gromov扭曲L2指标定理产生一族小酉扭转下的调和旋量；通过精化的Kato等式缺陷的共形解释分析等式情形；利用调和旋量构造共形相关度量下的平行旋量。

Result: 证明了闭Riemannian自旋流形上双曲标量曲率与万有覆盖谱下确界的尖锐比较；等式成立时原始度量是Einstein的；在正谱情形下，万有覆盖为实双曲空间。

Abstract: We study Gromov's exact-lift two-form method in scalar-curvature geometry. For a closed Riemannian spin manifold carrying a homologically non-trivial closed two-form whose lift to the universal cover is exact, we prove the sharp hyperbolic scalar-curvature comparison with the bottom of the spectrum of the universal Riemannian covering. The two-form enters through Gromov's twisted \(L^2\)-index, which produces harmonic spinors for a family of small unitary twists. We analyze the equality case by interpreting the refined Kato equality defect conformally and use the harmonic spinors to construct a parallel spinor with respect to a suitable conformally related metric. This yields that the original metric is Einstein. In the positive-spectrum case, this method implies that the universal cover is real hyperbolic.

### [52] [Some constructions of uniformly positive scalar curvature metrics on open manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19619)
*Anushree Das*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了开流形上的一致正数量曲率完备黎曼度量的多种构造。对于维数n≥3，若流形存在有界下方且无≥n-2指标临界点的恰当Morse函数，则存在一致正数量曲率度量；若流形存在正数量曲率度量及每个边界为极小的紧穷竭，则同样存在。对于4≤n≤7，若流形具有乘积末端及C-二次衰减（C>4π²）的正数量曲率度量，则远离基点的平均凸超曲面可导出一致正数量曲率度量。文章还研究了这些结果的应用，包括刻画无一致正数量曲率度量的开流形的末端结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在开流形上构造一致正数量曲率（UPSC）度量是几何分析中的重要问题。已有的正数量曲率（PSC）度量存在性结果较多，但一致正数量曲率（即曲率有严格正下界）的构造更为困难。本文旨在通过拓扑（Morse函数）和几何（极小时空、平均凸/凹超曲面）条件，给出UPSC度量的系统构造方法，并揭示PSC与UPSC之间的深层联系。

Method: （1）利用Morse理论，通过控制临界点指标（<n-2）构造UPSC度量； （2）利用极小边界穷竭，结合PSC度量的变形得到UPSC度量； （3）对于4≤n≤7，利用乘积末端结构和C-二次衰减条件（C>4π²），通过平均凸超曲面构造截断并配以标准度量的变形得到UPSC度量； （4）应用上述结果，通过反证法和已构造的UPSC度量，推导无UPSC流形的末端几何性质（平均凸/凹叶状结构）。

Result: （1）n≥3时，若开流形存在无≥n-2指标临界点的有界下方恰当Morse函数，则存在UPSC度量； （2）n≥3时，若开流形有PSC度量且存在极小边界穷竭，则存在UPSC度量； （3）4≤n≤7时，若开流形有乘积末端、PSC度量且满足C>4π²的二次衰减条件，则远离基点的平均凸超曲面可导出一致正数量曲率度量； （4）n≥3时，若无UPSC度量的开流形有PSC度量及平均凸穷竭，则末端存在平均凸叶状结构；若有平均凹穷竭，则末端存在平均凹叶状结构。

Conclusion: 本文建立了开流形上一致正数量曲率度量的多种构造方案，将拓扑条件（Morse临界点指标）与几何条件（极小时空、平均凸超曲面、二次衰减）统一在UPSC构造的框架下。同时，这些构造揭示了PSC度量与UPSC度量之间的本质差异——后者对末端几何有更强的约束（如叶状结构的存在性），为后续研究开流形正数量曲率问题提供了新的工具和视角。

Abstract: We obtain several constructions of uniformly positive scalar curvature complete Riemannian metrics on open manifolds. For dimension $n\geq3$, we show that if such a manifold admits a proper Morse function $f$ bounded below such that $f$ has no critical points of index $\geq n-2$, then it admits a uniformly positive scalar curvature metric. On the other hand if such a manifold admits a positive scalar curvature metric along with a compact exhaustion $\{U_i\}$ such that the boundary of each $U_i$ is minimal, then it also admits a uniformly positive scalar curvature metric. For dimension $4 \leq n\leq 7$, we show that if the manifold has product ends and a positive scalar curvature metric with $C$-quadratic decay at infinity for $C>4π^2$ with respect to some basepoint, then the existence of a mean convex hypersurface far enough from the basepoint implies the existence of a uniformly positive scalar curvature metric on the manifold. We study some applications of these results, including showing that if an open manifold of dimension $n\geq 3$ that admits no uniformly positive scalar curvature metric has a positive scalar curvature metric with mean convex exhaustion, then it admits a mean convex foliation of compact sets sufficiently close to the ends. On the other hand, if such a manifold has a mean concave exhaustion, then its ends admit a mean concave foliation.

</details>

Abstract: Our goal is to survey the development of positive mass theorem and the Yamabe equation on CR manifolds in recent years. We introduce the notion of the mass in several complex variables or CR geometry. We then consider the Yamabe problem on CR manifolds to find a minimizer for the CR-Sobolev quotient. The positive mass theorem plays a key role in finding a solution to the Yamabe equation with minimum energy for the positive curvature case. We mainly focus on the team works in the following three papers [CMY17], [CMY23] and [CC22], on a positive mass theorem in 3-dimensional CR geometry, the CR-Sobolev quotient of Rossi spheres, and the 5-dimensional situation, respectively.

### [54] [The top Yau--Yang conjecture for Kähler manifolds with positive sectional curvature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19806)
*Ved V. Datar,Vamsi P. Pingali,Harish Seshadri*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文证明了具有正截面曲率的完备非紧Kähler流形的Ricci形式最高楔积具有有限积分，并利用Chen-Zhu的结果，在截面曲率有界假设下推出此类流形的拟射影性。证明的关键新思想是使用具有有限Monge-Ampère质量的Lipschitz权函数来建立Bézout估计。

Method: 引入了具有有限Monge-Ampère质量的Lipschitz权函数，结合Bézout估计来证明主要结果。

Result: 证明了Ricci形式最高楔积在正截面曲率完备非紧Kähler流形上的积分有限；在截面曲率有界条件下，结合Chen-Zhu的结果推出该流形是拟射影的。

Conclusion: 正截面曲率条件对Kähler流形的几何与分析性质有深刻约束，其Ricci曲率的相关积分有限性可用于推断流形的代数几何结构（拟射影性）。

Abstract: We prove that the top wedge power of the Ricci form of a complete non-compact Kähler manifold with positive sectional curvature has finite integral. Using a result of Chen-Zhu, an immediate consequence is the quasiprojectivity of such manifolds under the assumption of bounded sectional curvature. A key new idea to prove Bézout estimates along with a Lipschitz weight with finite Monge-Ampère mass is used in the proof of the main result.

### [56] [Poisson and Jacobi structures from 2-covariant tensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20030)

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一框架，通过研究由非退化2-协变张量诱导的Poisson和Jacobi结构，推导了Schouten-Nijenhuis括号的计算公式，该公式以某分布的曲率和微分形式的外微分给出了Poisson或Jacobi结构存在的障碍，并恢复了辛、局部共形辛、余辛和接触几何中的经典括号，最后刻画了fat丛和p阶几乎余辛结构确定Jacobi括号的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Poisson和Jacobi结构在经典力学中具有基础性作用，通常由非退化2-协变张量诱导。作者希望建立一个统一框架来构造这些张量诱导的括号，并系统研究其存在性条件。

Method: 在张量的适当假设下，推导了关联双向量场的Schouten-Nijenhuis括号的计算公式，将其表示为某分布的曲率与微分形式的外微分的组合，以此作为Poisson或Jacobi结构存在的障碍条件。

Result: 获得了Poisson或Jacobi结构存在的障碍公式；恢复了辛、局部共形辛、余辛和接触几何中的经典括号；刻画了fat丛和p阶几乎余辛结构确定Jacobi括号的充要条件。

Conclusion: 该框架统一了多种几何结构，并为判断给定张量是否能诱导Poisson或Jacobi结构提供了系统的判别准则。

Abstract: Poisson and Jacobi structures play a fundamental role in the geometric description of many systems arising in classical mechanics. In most cases, the corresponding bivector field is induced by a non-degenerate 2-covariant tensor. In this paper, we present a unified framework for constructing the associated brackets by studying the Poisson and Jacobi structures induced by these tensors. More specifically, under suitable assumptions on the tensor, we derive a formula for computing the Schouten-Nijenhuis bracket of the associated bivector field in terms of the curvature of a certain distribution and the exterior derivative of a differential form. This formula provides the obstruction to the existence of a Poisson or Jacobi structure. To illustrate the theory, we recover the classical brackets associated with symplectic, locally conformally symplectic, cosymplectic, and contact geometries. Finally, we characterize the conditions under which fat bundles and almost cosymplectic structures of order $p$ determine a Jacobi bracket.

*Peng Peng*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Mean curvature flow is a fundamental geometric evolution equation in which a submanifold moves in the normal direction with velocity equal to its mean curvature vector. Self-shrinkers arise naturally as self-similar solutions to the mean curvature flow and play an important role as models for finite-time singularities. Among nontrivial examples of compact embedded self-shrinkers, the rotationally symmetric self-shrinking torus constructed by Angenent is one of the most important. However, the uniqueness of the Angenent torus remains a major open problem.

We analyze the profile curves of rotationally symmetric self-shrinkers, focusing on the behavior of their vertical points and the curves traced out by these points as the initial height varies. We give a new proof of the existence of the Angenent torus by showing that two families of vertical-point trajectories must intersect.
  We further derive the linearized equation associated with the rotationally symmetric self-shrinker equation and apply a Sturm-type comparison theorem to obtain sufficient conditions for the monotonicity of horizontal-point trajectories. In particular, we prove a comparison theorem for solutions near the spherical self-shrinker $x^{2}+r^{2}=2n$, and establish partial monotonicity results for the curves of horizontal points. ### [59] [The alignment time function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20481)
*Marco van den Beld-Serrano*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究在稳定因果时空中，给定一个过去指向的类时向量场，是否存在一个时间函数，其梯度与该向量场最优对齐。通过引入一个同时捕捉类时向量场与Sobolev函数梯度之间错位并惩罚零梯度的泛函，证明了在适当的Sobolev指数和零梯度惩罚强度下，存在唯一光滑的时间函数最小化该泛函，称为"对齐时间函数"，并建立了其陡度提升、稳定性及对称性继承等性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核心动机是解决"给定一个固定的过去指向类时向量场，是否存在一个时间函数使其梯度与该向量场最优对齐"这一基本问题。该问题本质上是将给定的类时向量场与某个时间函数的梯度进行最佳匹配，这对于理解时空结构具有重要意义。

Method: 方法上，作者引入了一个泛函，该泛函一方面衡量类时向量场与Sobolev函数梯度之间的错位，另一方面惩罚零梯度。在光滑稳定因果时空的紧子集上，在适当的Sobolev指数和零梯度惩罚强度假设下，证明了存在唯一的光滑时间函数最小化该泛函。

Result: 主要结果包括：(1) 存在唯一光滑的时间函数（对齐时间函数）最小化所提出的泛函；(2) 存在规范化的陡度提升程序；(3) 对齐时间函数在C^p收敛意义下对底层度规和向量场稳定；(4) 对齐时间函数继承度规和给定向量场的对称性。

Conclusion: 成功地建立了在稳定因果时空中，给定类时向量场与时间函数梯度之间的最优对齐理论，证明了对齐时间函数的存在性、唯一性、光滑性、稳定性及对称性继承等关键性质，为相关研究提供了有力的数学工具。

Abstract: Given a fixed past-directed timelike vector field, does there exist a time function whose gradient is optimally aligned with it? We address this question by introducing a functional that, on the one hand, captures the misalignment between the timelike vector field and the gradients of suitable Sobolev functions, and, on the other hand, penalizes null gradients. Our analysis focuses on compact subsets of smooth stably causal spacetimes. More precisely, we prove that, under suitable assumptions on the Sobolev index and the strength of the null gradient penalization, there exists a unique smooth temporal function which minimizes the considered functional. We refer to this minimizer as the \emph{alignment time function}. Furthermore, several useful properties of the alignment time function are established: there exists a canonical procedure to improve its steepness, it is stable under $C^{p}$ convergence of the underlying metrics and vector fields and it inherits the symmetries shared by the metric and the given vector field.

### [62] [Bootstrapping Pion Form Factors at Large $N$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19420)
*Jan Albert,Dilara Kosva,Leonardo Rastelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在大N QCD中对π介子形状因子进行自举研究，通过分析矢量流两点函数、π介子矢量形状因子和π介子散射振幅的混合系统，利用解析性、幺正性、交叉对称性和Regge有界性等谱数据约束，得到了两类界限：一是基于解析性、幺正性和Brodsky-Farrar渐近标度的普适严格界限；二是类似Shifman-Vainshtein-Zakharov型的唯象界限，通过输入有限能标处的微扰紫外行为来约束π介子衰变常数、电荷半径等低能参数。这些结果展示了局域规范不变探针如何在强子自举和微观QCD拉格朗日量之间建立规范桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 得到两类界限：1) 基于解析性和幺正性的普适界限，约束低能形状因子系数；2) 基于微扰紫外输入的唯象界限，可约束π介子衰变常数、将大N格点测量转化为渐近自由能标的下界、以及约束π介子电荷半径。这些输入使允许的手征拉格朗日量空间收缩至大N QCD预期区域。

Conclusion: 局域规范不变探针为强子自举与微观QCD拉格朗日量之间提供了规范桥梁，阐明了如何从第一性原理和微扰输入自洽地约束低能强子物理。

Abstract: We initiate a bootstrap study of pion form factors in large $N$ QCD. We consider the mixed system of the vector-current two-point function, the pion vector form factor, and the pion scattering amplitude in the chiral limit. At large $N$ these observables are meromorphic, with spectral data constrained by unitarity, crossing symmetry, and Regge boundedness. We obtain bounds of two kinds. The first are rigorous and universal: from analyticity, unitarity and the asymptotic Brodsky-Farrar scaling, we constrain low-energy form-factor coefficients. The second are more phenomenological, of the Shifman-Vainshtein-Zakharov type: feeding in the perturbative ultraviolet behavior at a finite scale lets us bound the pion decay constant, convert a large $N$ lattice measurement into a lower bound on the scale at which asymptotic freedom sets in, and constrain the pion charge radius. Combining these inputs, the space of allowed chiral Lagrangians shrinks toward the region where large $N$ QCD is expected to sit. Our results illustrate how local gauge-invariant probes provide a canonical bridge between the hadronic bootstrap and the microscopic QCD Lagrangian.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的弦紧致化模型大多假设额外维是各向同性的，而现实物理中可能需要各向异性的大额外维（如ADD情景中的两个大额外维，或Dark Dimension情景中的一个超大额外维）。本文旨在提供一个统一的模稳定化框架，在IIB弦论中实现这些各向异性紧致化，并确保模型在现象学上自洽。

Method: 采用Type IIB大体积场景（LVS），选择K3纤维化于ℙ^1基底的Calabi-Yau三维流形。通过微扰修正（弦圈效应和高阶导数效应）将4D K3纤维体积稳定在较小值，而2D ℙ^1基底的体积指数级大。复结构模稳定化动态变形ℙ^1基底，对应Tyurin退化极限，使得内部几何自发产生一个大的一维循环。ADD情景作为对称的替代极限恢复。势能可产生dS真空或quintessence逃逸。给出了具体的Calabi-Yau orientifold例子，包含一致的膜配置、tadpole抵消和模稳定化。

Result: 成功实现了各向异性弦紧致化：K3纤维体积小，ℙ^1基底体积指数级大，从而自然产生一维或二维大额外维。得到了相应的模谱，分析了超对称破缺尺度、宇宙学模过产生和第五力等现象学约束。但匹配观测到的宇宙学常数尺度需要一定程度的调谐。

Conclusion: 该工作为在弦论中实现各向异性大额外维（ADD和Dark Dimension）提供了自洽且统一的模稳定化机制，并指出这些情景在现象学上受到模稳定化细节的强大约束，为未来更现实的弦构建提供了指导。

Abstract: We provide a moduli stabilisation mechanism for realising anisotropic string compactifications with one or two large extra dimensions, corresponding to the ADD and Dark Dimension scenarios. This is achieved within the type IIB Large Volume Scenario, where an exponentially large Calabi-Yau volume in string units can naturally generate a parametrically low Kaluza-Klein scale. Anisotropy is realised by considering a Calabi-Yau threefold which is a K3 fibration over a $\mathbb{P}^1$ base. The volume of the 4D K3 fibre is stabilised at relatively small values by perturbative corrections to the effective action, in particular string loops and higher-derivative effects, leaving an exponentially large volume of the 2D $\mathbb{P}^1$ base. We argue that complex structure moduli stabilisation can dynamically deform the $\mathbb{P}^1$ base, corresponding to a Tyurin degeneration limit where the internal geometry effectively develops a single large 1D cycle. Within a unified description, the ADD case is instead recovered as a symmetric alternative limit. The potential can feature either a dS vacuum or a quintessence runaway, although in both cases some degree of tuning is required to match the observed cosmological constant scale. We also present an explicit Calabi-Yau orientifold example with consistent brane setup, tadpole cancellation and moduli stabilisation. We analyse the resulting moduli spectrum and associated phenomenological constraints, including supersymmetry breaking, cosmological moduli overproduction and fifth force bounds.

</details>

When $\mathrm{Y}_7$ is Sasaki-Einstein, we identify a special class of BPS M2-branes that preserve both real internal Killing spinors and correspond to invariant three-dimensional submanifolds inheriting a Sasakian structure. We analyse the quadratic fluctuations around BPS M2-brane instantons in these backgrounds. We then apply the index formula for the one-loop partition function to invariant M2-branes in $S^{7}/\mathbb{Z}_{k}$, recovering the known result for the $S^3/\mathbb{Z}_k$ instantons and discussing more general invariant BPS cycles. Method: 运用态-算符对应识别临界点并计算最低算符的标度维度；对Schwinger模型使用玻色化，对其他模型使用Polyakov-Hubbard变换，将临界点统一映射为带iφ³相互作用的玻色场理论；数值计算φ的两点关联函数。

Abstract: In this article, we present four different $1+1$D quantum models that realize the Yang-Lee (YL) phase transition under a deformation that preserves $PT$ symmetry. These are the antiferromagnetic Ising spin chain in transverse and longitudinal magnetic fields, the massive Schwinger model, the Blume-Capel model, and the three-state quantum clock model. Using the state-operator correspondence, we identify the YL critical point, compute the scaling dimensions of the lowest operators in each model, and find perfect agreement with the exact results for the YL criticality in two dimensions. Using bosonization for the Schwinger model and the Polyakov-Hubbard transformation for the other models, we show that in all of these quantum models the YL critical point is described, as expected, by a massless bosonic field with an $i φ^3$ interaction. In the quantum clock model, this critical field interacts with a massive bosonic field, and we identify the massless and massive states in the Hamiltonian spectrum. In addition, we numerically compute the two-point function of $φ$ at the Yang-Lee critical point and show that it grows with distance, in agreement with theoretical expectations.

Abstract: We revisit the Coleman--Weinberg monopole problem introduced by Kiselev, where radiative symmetry breaking makes the broken vacuum metastable. The monopole--bubble solution carries a negative radial mode, while the metastable monopole remains locally stable until its lowest radial Hessian eigenvalue approaches zero. ### [72] [Quantization of Brane-Skyrmions via Physics-Informed Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20066)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用(同位)旋集体坐标量子化方法，对哈密顿量进行J²幂次展开的微扰求解；引入物理信息神经网络(PINN)在考虑量子自旋反作用效应下求解能量最小化的孤子轮廓。

Result: 成功实现了Brane-Skyrmions的正则量子化，获得了可微扰求解的哈密顿量形式；PINN方法有效解决了含自旋反作用的孤子轮廓优化问题。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the canonical quantization of topological solitons appearing in braneworld scenarios. In particular, we focus on Brane-Skyrmions, topological field configurations analogous to standard Skyrmions, which emerge as solutions of the Dirac-Nambu-Goto action supplemented by an induced curvature term. By quantizing the (iso)spin collective coordinates of the Brane-Skyrmion, we obtain a Hamiltonian that we solve perturbatively via an expansion in powers of $J^2$, in contrast to the standard Skyrme model. Furthermore, we implement a Physics-Informed Neural Network (PINN) to determine the soliton profile that minimizes the energy, consistently incorporating the backreaction from the quantized spin degrees of freedom. We conclude with a discussion of the potential applications of this framework to the description of hadronic spectra. Our results highlight both the theoretical potential of brane-defect models and the growing role of neural network methods in theoretical physics.

</details>

### [74] [Macroscopic Black-Hole Remnants in a Nonlocal Field Theory: Towards Hawking Radiation in SFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20314)

Result: 早期时间（$u \ll u_{\text{scr}}$）再现霍金温度下的标准普朗克谱；而在混沌时间 $u_{\text{scr}}$ 之后不久，粒子数趋于零，辐射终止。

Conclusion: 霍金辐射在混沌时间附近因弦场论的非局域效应而提前终止，坍缩壳对超普朗克模式变得不可见，从而以宏观遗迹形式解决信息悖论。

Abstract: We demonstrate that, for a large black hole of radius $a$, Hawking radiation terminates around the scrambling time $u_{\text{scr}} \equiv 2a \log(a/\ell)$ due to the nonlocal, exponential suppression of trans-Planckian interactions inherent in string field theory (SFT). Modifying a massless scalar field's interaction with a dynamical black hole background via the smearing operator $e^{\ell^2\Box}$ (where $\ell$ denotes the string length scale), we calculate the time-dependent number expectation value $\langle \hat{N}(u) \rangle$ of outgoing Hawking particles at retarded time $u$. While the standard Planck spectrum at the Hawking temperature is reproduced at early times ($u \ll u_{\text{scr}}$), the particle number approaches zero shortly after the scrambling time. This early shutoff reflects the property that the collapsing shell becomes effectively invisible to trans-Planckian modes, offering an alternative resolution to the black hole information paradox via a macroscopic remnant.

The Hamiltonian of the model is completely local, but the vacuum exhibits correlations among planck scale fluctuations which fall off relatively slowly with distance. We calculate the action of the supercharges in the sector $(h,j)=(1,0)$ for different values of the central charge and derive explicit expressions for the primary states. Abstract: We argue that celestial OPEs must be supplemented by shadow-basis operators. From OPE consistency, we show that the ordinary celestial OPE does not close on Mellin-basis exchanges alone. Rather, the same exchanged bulk particle must also appear through its shadow-basis representative. This leads to a shadow-completed OPE, with the shadow OPE coefficient fixed by the ordinary collinear coefficient through the universal shadow factor. We discuss the corresponding boundary Hilbert-space interpretation, extend this argument to gluons and gravitons, and verify the shadow exchange directly in tree-level regular celestial amplitudes, including a scalar $2\rightarrow n$ analysis and an explicit five-point example.

Assuming a stabilisation mechanism of the extra dimensions at the end of inflation, here we propose a cosmological history that describes the Universe evolution after the end of inflation up to the reheating temperature, that guarantees the absence of bulk gravitons at earlier times, avoiding their overproduction in the early universe. Abstract: We present for the first time the exact solution of the massive Klein-Gordon equation in the Schwarzschild star (perfect-fluid, uniform-density, spherically-symmetric star), including the non-minimal curvature-scalar coupling. Known leading- and next-to-leading-order results are recovered in the low-compactness limit. Abstract: We investigate top-down derivations of effective descriptions for radiation from gravitational systems such as binaries. With a specified cutoff prescription, one can derive worldline effective field theories, but the cutoff dependence also complicates their description. We investigate a related effective approach, based on parameterizing dynamics in terms of an action on the boundaries of cavities encompassing individual bodies. We give examples of such cavity descriptions for black holes and for simple models for modifications of their behavior. We also show how cavity effective descriptions connect to observable quantities -- detailed wave profiles, and importantly, accumulated phase shift of emitted signals. A primary motivation is to have a systematic approach to inferring effects of modification of classical black hole behavior, such as those motivated by the need for black hole evolution to be consistent with quantum mechanics, or by other models for new BH behavior, on gravitational wave signals; the latter phase shifts have in particular been argued to provide sensitivity to small new effects from the inspiral phase.
